      "code": "import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport { Box, TextField, Button, Typography, Avatar, Paper } from '@mui/material';\nimport SendIcon from '@mui/icons-material/Send';\nimport SmartToyIcon from '@mui/icons-material/SmartToy';\nimport api from '../../api';\nimport '../../styles/App.css';\n\nexport default function ChatInterface() {\n    const [message, setMessage] = useState('');\n    const [conversation, setConversation] = useState([]);\n    const messagesEndRef = useRef(null);\n\n    const loadConversation = async () => {\n        try {\n            const response = await api.getConversation();\n            setConversation(response.data.messages);\n        } catch (error) {\n            setConversation([{ role: 'assistant', content: '\u00a1Hola! Soy Coder, Puedo ayudarte a entender, depurar y mejorar tu c\u00f3digo. Preg\u00fantame sobre funciones, errores, refactorizaci\u00f3n o cualquier duda t\u00e9cnica.', timestamp: new Date() }]);\n        }\n    };\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        loadConversation();\n    }, []); \n\n\n    const handleSend = async () => {\n        if (!message) return;\n\n        const messageWritten = message;\n        setMessage('');\n\n        const newMessage = { role: 'user', content: messageWritten, timestamp: new Date() };\n        setConversation((prev) => [...prev, newMessage]);\n\n        try {\n            const response = await api.sendMessage({ message: messageWritten });\n            const aiMessage = {\n                role: 'assistant',\n                content: response.data.response,\n                timestamp: new Date()\n            };\n            setConversation((prev) => [...prev, aiMessage]);\n        } catch (error) {\n            setConversation((prev) => prev.slice(0, -1));\n        }\n        setMessage('');\n    };\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth'});\n    }, [conversation]);\n\n    return (\n        <Box className=\"chat-container\">\n            {/* Chat Messages */}\n            <Box className=\"chat-messages\">\n                {conversation.map((msg, index) => (\n                    <Box\n                        key={index}\n                        className={`chat-message ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'user' : 'assistant'}`}\n                    >\n                        <Typography variant=\"body1\">{msg.content}</Typography>\n                        <hr />\n                        <Typography variant=\"caption\" sx={{ color: '#ffffff86' }}>\n                        {new Date(msg.timestamp).toDateString().split(' ')[2]} {new Date(msg.timestamp).toDateString().split(' ')[1]}, {new Date(msg.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: \"2-digit\", minute: \"2-digit\" })}\n                        </Typography>\n                    </Box>\n                ))}\n                <div ref={messagesEndRef} />\n            </Box>\n\n            {/* Message Input */}\n            <Paper className=\"chat-input\" elevation={1} sx={{display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'row', boxShadow: 'none'}}>\n                <TextField\n                    fullWidth\n                    variant=\"outlined\"\n                    placeholder=\"Type your message...\"\n                    value={message}\n                    onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}\n                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}\n                />\n                <Button\n                    variant=\"contained\"\n                    onClick={handleSend}\n                    disabled={!message}\n                    endIcon={<SendIcon />}\n                >\n                </Button>\n            </Paper>\n        </Box>\n    );\n}",

// Assuming this endpoint exists\n        setUser(response.data.account);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n  \n    const login = async (email, password) => {\n        const response = await API.login({ email, password }); // Assuming this endpoint exists\n        // Assuming the token is stored and used for authenticated requests\n        const { token, user: loggedInUser } = response.data;\n        axios.defaults.headers.common['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;\n        setUser(loggedInUser);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        localStorage.setItem('token', token);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n\n    const value = {\n        user,\n        email,\n        signUp,\n        login,\n        logout,\n    };\n\n    return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;\n};",

    "contenido": {
      "code": "import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';\nimport axios from 'axios';\nimport API from '../api';\n\nconst AuthContext = createContext();\n\n\n\nexport const useAuth = () => {\n    return useContext(AuthContext);\n};\n\nexport const AuthProvider = ({ children }) => {\n    const [user, setUser] = useState(null);\n    const [email, setEmail] = useState(localStorage.getItem('userEmail') || '');\n    \n    useEffect(() => {\n        const token = localStorage.getItem('token');\n        if (token) {\n            axios.defaults.headers.common['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;\n            // Optionally, you can fetch the user data here if needed\n            // For example:\n            // API.getUser().then(response => setUser(response.data.user)).catch(error => console.error(error));\n        }\n    }, []);\n\n    const logout = () => {\n        localStorage.removeItem('userEmail');\n        localStorage.removeItem('token');\n        setEmail('');\n        setUser(null);\n        delete axios.defaults.headers.common['Authorization'];\n    };\n\n    const signUp = async (email, password, username) => {\n        const response = await API.createAccount({ email, password, username }); // Assuming this endpoint exists\n        setUser(response.data.account);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n  \n    const login = async (email, password) => {\n        const response = await API.login({ email, password }); // Assuming this endpoint exists\n        // Assuming the token is stored and used for authenticated requests\n        const { token, user: loggedInUser } = response.data;\n        axios.defaults.headers.common['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;\n        setUser(loggedInUser);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        localStorage.setItem('token', token);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n\n    const value = {\n        user,\n        email,\n        signUp,\n        login,\n        logout,\n    };\n\n    return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;\n};",

// Assuming this endpoint exists\n        setUser(response.data.account);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n  \n    const login = async (email, password) => {\n        const response = await API.login({ email, password }); // Assuming this endpoint exists\n        setUser(response.data.account);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n  \n    const login = async (email, password) => {\n        const response = await API.login({ email, password }); // Assuming this endpoint exists\n        // Assuming the token is stored and used for authenticated requests\n        const { token, user: loggedInUser } = response.data;\n        axios.defaults.headers.common['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;\n        setUser(loggedInUser);\n        localStorage.setItem('userEmail', email);\n        localStorage.setItem('token', token);\n        setEmail(email);\n        return response.data;\n    };\n\n    const value = {\n        user,\n        email,\n        signUp,\n        login,\n        logout,\n    };\n\n    return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;\n};",

      "code": "import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport { Box, TextField, Button, Typography, Avatar, Paper } from '@mui/material';\nimport SendIcon from '@mui/icons-material/Send';\nimport SmartToyIcon from '@mui/icons-material/SmartToy';\nimport api from '../../api';\nimport '../../styles/App.css';\n\nexport default function ChatInterface() {\n    const [message, setMessage] = useState('');\n    const [conversation, setConversation] = useState([]);\n    const messagesEndRef = useRef(null);\n\n    const loadConversation = async () => {\n        try {\n            const response = await api.getConversation();\n            setConversation(response.data.messages);\n        } catch (error) {\n            setConversation([{ role: 'assistant', content: '\u00a1Hola! Soy Coder, Puedo ayudarte a entender, depurar y mejorar tu c\u00f3digo. Preg\u00fantame sobre funciones, errores, refactorizaci\u00f3n o cualquier duda t\u00e9cnica.', timestamp: new Date() }]);\n        }\n    };\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        loadConversation();\n    }, []); \n\n\n    const handleSend = async () => {\n        if (!message) return;\n\n        const messageWritten = message;\n        setMessage('');\n\n        const newMessage = { role: 'user', content: messageWritten, timestamp: new Date() };\n        setConversation((prev) => [...prev, newMessage]);\n\n        try {\n            const response = await api.sendMessage({ message: messageWritten });\n            const aiMessage = {\n                role: 'assistant',\n                content: response.data.response,\n                timestamp: new Date()\n            };\n            setConversation((prev) => [...prev, aiMessage]);\n        } catch (error) {\n            setConversation((prev) => prev.slice(0, -1));\n        }\n        setMessage('');\n    };\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth'});\n    }, [conversation]);\n\n    return (\n        <Box className=\"chat-container\">\n            {/* Chat Messages */}\n            <Box className=\"chat-messages\">\n                {conversation.map((msg, index) => (\n                    <Box\n                        key={index}\n                        className={`chat-message ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'user' : 'assistant'}`}\n                    >\n                        <Typography variant=\"body1\">{msg.content}</Typography>\n                        <hr />\n                        <Typography variant=\"caption\" sx={{ color: '#ffffff86' }}>\n                        {new Date(msg.timestamp).toDateString().split(' ')[2]} {new Date(msg.timestamp).toDateString().split(' ')[1]}, {new Date(msg.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: \"2-digit\", minute: \"2-digit\" })}\n                        </Typography>\n                    </Box>\n                ))}\n                <div ref={messagesEndRef} />\n            </Box>\n\n            {/* Message Input */}\n            <Paper className=\"chat-input\" elevation={1} sx={{display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'row', boxShadow: 'none'}}>\n                <TextField\n                    fullWidth\n                    variant=\"outlined\"\n                    placeholder=\"Type your message...\"\n                    value={message}\n                    onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}\n                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}\n                />\n                <Button\n                    variant=\"contained\"\n                    onClick={handleSend}\n                    disabled={!message}\n                    endIcon={<SendIcon />}\n                >\n                </Button>\n            </Paper>\n        </Box>\n    );\n}",
